### Try to keep tags in alphabetical order if it's not too far gone, please.

## DEFAULT COUNTRY NAMES EXAMPLE CAN BE USED WITH ANY COUNTRY ##

# Uncomment when need a dynamic_country_name for any country
DEFAULT = {
	# ACW revolters
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = csa_revolt_name
		adjective = csa_revolt_name_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = c:CSA
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				this = c:CSA
			}
		}
	}
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = fsa_revolt_name
		adjective = fsa_revolt_name_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = c:FSA
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				this = c:FSA
			}
		}
	}
	# Important ideologies
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = generic_revolt_communist
		adjective = generic_revolt_communist_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				is_secessionist = no
				any_interest_group = {
					is_in_government = yes
					is_powerful = yes
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology_communist
							has_ideology = ideology_anarchist
							has_ideology = ideology_vanguardist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = generic_revolt_fascist
		adjective = generic_revolt_fascist_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				is_secessionist = no
				any_interest_group = {
					is_in_government = yes
					leader = {
						OR = {
							has_ideology = ideology_fascist
							has_ideology = ideology_ethno_nationalist
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = generic_revolt_radical
		adjective = generic_revolt_radical_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				is_secessionist = no
				any_interest_group = {
					is_in_government = yes
					leader = {
						has_ideology = ideology_radical
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	# Powerful interest groups
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = generic_revolt_peasant
		adjective = generic_revolt_peasant_adj
		
		is_revolutionary = yes
		priority = 0

			scope:actor = {
				is_secessionist = no
				ig:ig_rural_folk = {
					is_powerful = yes
					is_in_government = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	dynamic_country_name = {

ABS = { # Apsáalooke
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_decentralized
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_decentralized_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			scope:actor = {
				is_country_type = decentralized
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_theocracy
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_theocracy_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			coa_def_theocracy_flag_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_monarchy
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_monarchy_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					coa_def_absolute_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
					coa_def_undemocratic_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
					coa_def_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
				}
				scope:actor = {
					NOT = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_fascist
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_fascist_adj

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			coa_def_fascist_flag_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_dictatorship
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_dictatorship_adj

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				coa_def_dictatorship_flag_trigger = yes
				coa_def_military_junta_flag_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_communist
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_communist_adj

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			coa_def_communist_flag_trigger = yes
		}
	}

	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ABS_republic
		adjective = dyn_c_ABS_republic_adj

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			AND = {

				coa_def_anarchy_flag_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {

ACE = { # Aceh
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_sumatra
		adjective = dyn_c_sumatra_adj
		
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			exists = scope:actor
			scope:actor = {
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_ACEH
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_NORTH_SUMATRA
				owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SOUTH_SUMATRA
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_ACE_Sumatra_theocracy
		adjective = dyn_c_ACE_Sumatra_theocracy_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes

		trigger = {
			AND = {
				coa_def_theocracy_flag_trigger = yes
				scope:actor = {
					AND = {
						owns_entire_state_region = STATE_ACEH
						owns_entire_state_region = STATE_NORTH_SUMATRA
						owns_entire_state_region = STATE_SOUTH_SUMATRA
					}
				}
			}
		}

	dynamic_country_name = {

					coa_def_undemocratic_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
					coa_def_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes

					AND = {
						NOT = {
							is_country_type = decentralized

		name = dyn_c_BIC_Raj
		adjective = dyn_c_BIC_Raj_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 1
		
		trigger = {
			exists = c:GBR
			c:GBR = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:BIC
					type = puppet
					is_initiator = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_BIC_company
		adjective = dyn_c_BIC_company_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 1
		
		trigger = {
			exists = c:GBR
			c:GBR = {
				has_diplomatic_pact = {
					who = c:BIC
					type = dominion
					is_initiator = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_BLA_theocracy
		adjective = dyn_c_BLA_theocracy_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			coa_def_theocracy_flag_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_BLA_monarchy
		adjective = dyn_c_BLA_monarchy_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				OR = {
					coa_def_absolute_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
					coa_def_undemocratic_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
					coa_def_monarchy_flag_trigger = yes
				}
				scope:actor = {
					NOT = {
						is_country_type = decentralized
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_BLA_fascist
		adjective = dyn_c_BLA_fascist_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

		name = dyn_c_BLA_dictatorship

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				coa_def_dictatorship_flag_trigger = yes

				}
			}
		}
	}

				coa_def_dictatorship_flag_trigger = yes
				coa_def_military_junta_flag_trigger = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_USA_communist
		adjective = dyn_c_USA_communist_ADJ
		
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			coa_def_communist_flag_trigger = yes
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_USA_senators
		adjective = dyn_c_USA_senators_ADJ
		
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 1
		
		trigger = {
			exists = c:USA
			c:USA = {			
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = { 
						has_variable = district_of_columbia 
					}
					count > 0
				}
				any_scope_state = {
					state_region = { 
						NOT = { 
							has_variable = district_of_columbia 
						} 
					}
					count < 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	dynamic_country_name = {
		name = dyn_c_USA_republic
		adjective = dyn_c_USA_republic_ADJ

		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0
		
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				coa_def_republic_flag_trigger = yes
				coa_def_anarchy_flag_trigger = no
			}
		}
	}

ZAI = { # Azal (Zaidi State)

		name = dyn_c_qasimid_state
		adjective = dyn_c_qasimid_state_adj
		
		is_main_tag_only = yes
		priority = 0

				}
			}
		}
	}
